Both the Inch and Centimeter measurement units are supported.\r\n\r\nThe app is capable of creating Code 39, Industrial 2 of 5 and POSTNET barcode using TrueType fonts. This is important for printing high quality barcode labels as it allows high resolution printing and produces barcodes that are sharp and accurate. The high resolution barcodes also ensures requirements of industry specifications such as those by GS1 and ISO can be met with ease.
